orchestrates complex workflows through LLM-powered task decomposition, parallel execution, and intelligent tool management. The system spans 137 Python files organized into core agent logic, tool ecosystem (40+ tools), web UI infrastructure, session/memory management, and platform integrations.\n                    </div>\n                </div>\n                <div class="card">\n                    <div class="card-title">Key Capabilities</div>\n                    <div class="card-content">\n                        ✓ Multi-provider LLM abstraction (OpenAI, Anthropic, Gemini, xAI, Ollama)<br>\n                        ✓ 40+ integrated tools for web, file, browser, and system operations<br>\n                        ✓ Real-time multi-client WebSocket communication<br>\n                        ✓ Token-aware context management and intelligent memory layers<br>\n                        ✓ Parallel task orchestration with dependency resolution<br>\n                        ✓ Platform integrations (Telegram, Discord, Slack, Google Workspace)\n                    </div>\n                </div>\n            </div>\n        </div>\n        \n        <!-- Key Statistics -->\n        <div class="section">\n            <h2 class="section-title">System Statistics</h2>\n            <div class="stats-grid">\n                <div class="stat-card">\n                    <div class="stat-number">137</div>\n                    <div class="stat-label">Python Files</div>\n                </div>\n                <div class="stat-card">\n                    <div class="stat-number">40+</div>\n                    <div class="stat-label">Integrated Tools</div>\n                </div>\n                <div class="stat-card">\n                    <div class="stat-number">13</div>\n                    <div class="stat-label">Agent Mixins</div>\n                </div>\n                <div class="stat-card">\n                    <div class="stat-number">50+</div>\n                    <div class="stat-label">REST Endpoints</div>\n                </div>\n            </div>\n        </div>\n        \n        <!-- Architecture Overview -->\n        <div class="section">\n            <h2 class="section-title">Architecture Overview</h2>\n            \n            <div class="subsection-title">Core Components</div>\n            <div class="diagram-container">\n                <div class="mermaid">\ngraph TB\n    subgraph "Agent Engine"\n        A[Agent Base Class]\n        A --> O["Orchestration Mixin<br/>(Turn Processing)"]\n        A --> T["Tool Loop Mixin<br/>(Execution)"]\n        A --> C["Completion Mixin<br/>(Validation)"]\n        A --> M["Context Mixin<br/>(Memory)"]\n        A --> S["Session Mixin<br/>(State)"]\n    end\n    \n    subgraph "Tool Ecosystem"\n        F["File Ops<br/>(read, write, glob)"]\n        W["Web Tools<br/>(fetch, search, browser)"]\n        D["Data Tools<br/>(datastore, typesense)"]\n        G["Google Tools<br/>(Drive, Docs, Calendar)"]\n        P["Productivity<br/>(todo, contacts, playbooks)"]\n    end\n    \n    subgraph "Memory Layers"\n        WM["Working Memory<br/>(in-turn)"]\n        SM["Semantic Memory<br/>(session-scoped)"]\n        DM["Deep Memory<br/>(long-term archive)"]\n    end\n    \n    subgraph "Web Infrastructure"\n        WS["WebSocket Handler"]\n        REST["REST API<br/>(50+ endpoints)"]\n        SP["Static Pages<br/>(23 templates)"]\n    end\n    \n    subgraph "Platform Integrations"\n        TG["Telegram"]\n        DC["Discord"]\n        SL["Slack"]\n        GW["Google Workspace"]\n    end\n    \n    A --> F\n    A --> W\n    A --> D\n    A --> G\n    A --> P\n    A --> WM\n    A --> SM\n    A --> DM\n    WS --> A\n    REST --> A\n    SP --> WS\n    TG --> A\n    DC --> A\n    SL --> A\n    GW --> A\n                </div>\n            </div>\n            \n            <div class="subsection-title">Agent Mixin Architecture</div>\n            <p style="margin-bottom: 20px; color: #cccccc;">The Agent class uses 13 specialized mixins providing distinct capabilities:</p>\n            \n            <table>\n                <thead>\n                    <tr>\n                        <th>Mixin</th>\n                        <th>Responsibility</th>\n                        <th>Key Features</th>\n                    </tr>\n                </thead>\n                <tbody>\n                    <tr>\n                        <td><strong>Orchestration</strong></td>\n                        <td>Main turn-level request processing loop</td>\n                        <td>Iteration budgets, progress tracking, completion gating</td>\n                    </tr>\n                    <tr>\n                        <td><strong>Tool Loop</strong></td>\n                        <td>LLM tool call extraction and execution</td>\n                        <td>Duplicate detection, scale-aware guards</td>\n                    </tr>\n                    <tr>\n                        <td><strong>Completion</strong></td>\n                        <td>Multi-stage validation gates</td>\n                        <td>Task requirement verification before finalization</td>\n                    </tr>\n                    <tr>\n                        <td><strong>Context</strong></td>\n                        <td>Dynamic system prompt construction</td>\n                        <td>Semantic memory integration, intelligent message selection</td>\n                    </tr>\n                    <tr>\n                        <td><strong>Session</strong></td>\n                        <td>Token-aware message handling</td>\n                        <td>Context compaction, runtime configuration sync</td>\n                    </tr>\n                    <tr>\n                        <td><strong>File Operations</strong></td>\n                        <td>Script generation and execution</td>\n                        <td>Structured result wrapping, artifact management</td>\n                    </tr>\n                    <tr>\n                        <td><strong>Guard</strong></td>\n                        <td>Input/output content filtering</td>\n                        <td>Approval workflows, safety gates</td>\n                    </tr>\n                    <tr>\n                        <td><strong>Model</strong></td>\n                        <td>Runtime model selection</td>\n                        <td>Provider resolution, multi-model support</td>\n                    </tr>\n                    <tr>\n                        <td><strong>Pipeline</strong></td>\n                        <td>DAG-based task decomposition</td>\n                        <td>Dependency resolution, timeout management</td>\n                    </tr>\n                    <tr>\n                        <td><strong>Reasoning</strong></td>\n                        <td>Task contract generation</td>\n                        <td>Critic validation, list extraction</td>\n                    </tr>\n                    <tr>\n                        <td><strong>Research</strong></td>\n                        <td>Multi-stage web research</td>\n                        <td>Entity extraction, content aggregation</td>\n                    </tr>\n                    <tr>\n                        <td><strong>Scale Detection</strong></td>\n                        <td>Large-scale task detection</td>\n                        <td>Advisory injection, list processing</td>\n                    </tr>\n                    <tr>\n                        <td><strong>Scale Loop</strong></td>\n                        <td>Per-item batch processing</td>\n                        <td>Constant-context isolation, incremental results</td>\n                    </tr>\n                </tbody>\n            </table>\n        </div>\n        \n        <!-- Tool Ecosystem -->\n        <div class="section">\n            <h2 class="section-title">Tool Ecosystem</h2>\n            <p style="margin-bottom: 30px; color: class="card-title">File & Text Operations</div>\n                    <ul class="feature-list">\n                        <li><strong>read.py</strong> — Safe file reading with path resolution</li>\n                        <li><strong>write.py</strong> — Sandboxed file writing with session scoping</li>\n                        <li><strong>edit.py</strong> — Surgical file editing with backup/undo</li>\n                        <li><strong>glob.py</strong> — Pattern-based file discovery</li>\n                    </ul>\n                </div>\n                \n                <div class="card">\n                    <div class="card-title">Web & Data Integration</div>\n                    <ul class="feature-list">\n                        <li><strong>web_fetch.py</strong> — HTTP content retrieval (text)</li>\n                        <li><strong>web_get.py</strong> — HTTP content retrieval (raw HTML)</li>\n                        <li><strong>web_search.py</strong> — Brave Search API integration</li>\n                        <li><strong>google_drive.py</strong> — Google Drive file operations</li>\n                        <li><strong>google_mail.py</strong> — Gmail read-only access</li>\n                        <li><strong>google_calendar.py</strong> — Calendar event management</li>\n                        <li><strong>typesense.py</strong> — Vector search & indexing</li>\n                        <li><strong>datastore.py</strong> — Relational database operations</li>\n                    </ul>\n                </div>\n                \n                <div class="card">\n                    <div class="card-title">Document Processing</div>\n                    <ul class="feature-list">\n                        <li><strong>document_extract.py</strong> — Multi-format extraction (PDF, DOCX, XLSX, PPTX)</li>\n                        <li><strong>image_ocr.py</strong> — OCR via vision models</li>\n                        <li><strong>image_gen.py</strong> — Image generation</li>\n                        <li><strong>summarize_files.py</strong> — Batch file summarization</li>\n                    </ul>\n                </div>\n                \n                <div class="card">\n                    <div class="card-title">Browser Automation</div>\n                    <ul class="feature-list">\n                        <li><strong>browser.py</strong> — Playwright-based browser with persistent sessions</li>\n                        <li><strong>pinchtab.py</strong> — Token-efficient accessibility tree automation</li>\n                        <li><strong>browser_workflow.py</strong> — Record-and-replay automation</li>\n                        <li><strong>browser_api_replay.py</strong> — Direct API execution from network captures</li>\n                        <li><strong>browser_credentials.py</strong> — Encrypted credential storage</li>\n                        <li><strong>browser_network.py</strong> — Network traffic interception</li>\n                    </ul>\n                </div>\n                \n                <div class="card">\n                    <div class="card-title">System & Hardware</div>\n                    <ul class="feature-list">\n                        <li><strong>shell.py</strong> — Secure shell command execution</li>\n                        <li><strong>desktop_action.py</strong> — GUI automation (mouse, keyboard)</li>\n                        <li><strong>screen_capture.py</strong> — Screenshot capture</li>\n                        <li><strong>clipboard.py</strong> — macOS clipboard operations</li>\n                        <li><strong>termux.py</strong> — Android device control</li>\n                        <li><strong>stt.py</strong> — Speech-to-text (multi-provider)</li>\n                        <li><strong>pocket_tts.py</strong> — Local text-to-speech</li>\n                    </ul>\n                </div>\n                \n                <div class="card">\n                    <div class="card-title">Productivity & Context</div>\n                    <ul class="feature-list">\n                        <li><strong>todo.py</strong> — Cross-session task management</li>\n                        <li><strong>contacts.py</strong> — Address book with importance scoring</li>\n                        <li><strong>scripts.py</strong> — Script registry with usage tracking</li>\n                        <li><strong>apis.py</strong> — API endpoint management</li>\n                        <li><strong>personality.py</strong> — Agent/user personality profiles</li>\n                        <li><strong>playbooks.py</strong> — Reusable task pattern library</li>\n                        <li><strong>send_mail.py</strong> — Email dispatch</li>\n                    </ul>\n                </div>\n            </div>\n        </div>\n        \n        <!-- Memory Architecture -->\n        <div class="section">\n            <h2 class="section-title">Memory Architecture</h2>\n            \n            <div class="grid-2">\n                <div class="card">\n                    <div class="card-title">Working Memory</div>\n                    <div class="card-content">\n                        In-turn context buffer with automatic compaction. Holds current conversation state and tool results within the LLM\'s context window. Implements sliding-window compression when token limits are approached.\n                    </div>\n                </div>\n                <div class="card">\n                    <div class="card-title">Semantic Memory</div>\n                    <div class="card-content">\n                        Session-scoped SQLite FTS5 + vector embeddings with hybrid search. Combines full-text search (BM25) with vector similarity and temporal decay scoring for intelligent context retrieval.\n                    </div>\n                </div>\n                <div class="card">\n                    <div class="card-title">Deep Memory</div>\n                    <div class="card-content">\n                        Typesense-backed long-term archive with chunking and embedding. Stores historical data across sessions for cross-session learning and reference.\n                    </div>\n                </div>\n                <div class="card">\n                    <div class="card-title">File Registry</div>\n                    <div class="card-content">\n                        Logical-to-physical path mapping for cross-task artifact discovery. Enables downstream tasks to reference upstream artifacts without knowledge of session IDs or directory structures.\n                    </div>\n                </div>\n            </div>\n        </div>\n        \n        <!-- LLM Provider Support -->\n        <div class="section">\n            <h2 class="section-title">Multi-Provider LLM Support</h2>\n            \n            <div class="chart-container chart-container-tall">\n                <canvas id="providerChart"></canvas>\n            </div>\n            \n            <div class="grid-2">\n                <div class="card">\n                    <div class="card-title">Supported Providers</div>\n                    <ul class="feature-list">\n                        <li><strong>OpenAI/ChatGPT</strong> — Standard API + ChatGPT Responses API (SSE streaming)</li>\n                        <li><strong>Anthropic Claude</strong> — With prompt caching support</li>\n                        <li><strong>Google Gemini</strong> — Via LiteLLM with async/sync handling</li>\n                        <li><strong>xAI Grok</strong> — Via LiteLLM</li>\n                        <li><strong>Ollama</strong> — Direct HTTP client for local models</li>\n                    </ul>\n                </div>\n                <div class="card">\n                    <div class="card-title">Advanced Features</div>\n                    <ul class="feature-list">\n                        <li>Token rate limiting with sliding-window backpressure</li>\n                        <li>Provider-specific message/tool conversion</li>\n                        <li>Unified tool definition schema</li>\n                        <li>Streaming response collection</li>\n                        <li>Token counting and usage tracking</li>\n                    </ul>\n                </div>\n            </div>\n        </div>\n        \n        <!-- Web Infrastructure -->\n        <div class="section">\n            <h2 class="section-title">Web Infrastructure</h2>\n            \n            <div class="subsection-title">Core Server Architecture</div>\n            <div class="grid-2">\n                <div class="card">\n                    <div class="card-title">aiohttp Web Server</div>\n                    <div class="card-content">\n                        Async web server with 100+ HTTP/WebSocket route handlers. Real-time callback routing to connected clients without tight coupling. Multi-session state management and third-party integration orchestration.\n                    </div>\n                </div>\n                <div class="card">\n                    <div class="card-title">WebSocket Communication</div>\n                    <div class="card-content">\n                        Real-time bidirectional communication for chat messages, session state sync, and live speech-to-text streaming. Supports concurrent task naming and agent execution feedback.\n                    </div>\n                </div>\n            </div>\n            \n            <div class="subsection-title">REST API Modules (50+ Endpoints)</div>\n            <ul class="feature-list" style="margin-left: 0;">\n                <li><strong>Session Management</strong> — List, create, switch, export sessions</li>\n                <li><strong>Entity CRUD</strong> — Todos, contacts, scripts, APIs, playbooks</li>\n                <li><strong>Datastore Operations</strong> — Table/row management, import/export</li>\n                <li><strong>Cron Jobs</strong> — Scheduling and execution</li>\n                <li><strong>File Browsing</strong> — Local and media serving</li>\n                <li><strong>Configuration</strong> — Management with hot-reload</li>\n                <li><strong>Orchestrator Control</strong> — Workflow management and execution</li>\n                <li><strong>Deep Memory</strong> — Search and indexing</li>\n                <li><strong>OAuth Authentication</strong> — Google Workspace integration</li>\n            </ul>\n        </div>\n        \n        <!-- Platform Integrations -->\n        <div class="section">\n            <h2 class="section-title">Platform Integrations</h2>\n            \n            <div class="grid-2">\n                <div class="card">\n                    <div class="card-title">Telegram Bridge</div>\n                    <div class="card-content">\n                        Per-user Agent instances with session isolation. User approval workflow with pairing tokens. Typing indicators and inline keyboards for next steps. Image upload/download support and slash command execution.\n                    </div>\n                </div>\n                <div class="card">\n                    <div class="card-title">Discord Bridge</div>\n                    <div class="card-content">\n                        DM-based polling interface with message normalization. Bot mention detection and audio file upload support. Lightweight integration for Discord communities.\n                    </div>\n                </div>\n                <div class="card">\n                    <div class="card-title">Slack Bridge</div>\n                    <div class="card-content">\n                        DM-first polling with pagination support. User caching and username resolution. Thread reply support for organized conversations.\n                    </div>\n                </div>\n                <div class="card">\n                    <div class="card-title">Google Workspace</div>\n                    <div class="card-content">\n                        PKCE-based OAuth authorization flow. Token lifecycle management and credential injection. Full integration with Drive, Docs, Sheets, Calendar, and Gmail.\n                    </div>\n                </div>\n            </div>\n        </div>\n        \n        <!-- Tool Distribution Chart -->\n        <div class="section">\n            <h2 class="section-title">Tool Distribution by Category</h2>\n            <div class="chart-container">\n                <canvas id="toolDistributionChart"></canvas>\n            </div>\n        </div>\n        \n        <!-- Key Design Patterns -->\n        <div class="section">\n            <h2 class="section-title">Key Design Patterns</h2>\n            \n            <div class="grid-2">\n                <div class="card">\n                    <div class="card-title">1. Mixin-Based Composition</div>\n                    <div class="card-content">\n                        The Agent class uses 13 mixins to provide distinct capabilities without deep inheritance hierarchies. Each mixin focuses on a specific concern, enabling modular testing and feature toggling.\n                    </div>\n                </div>\n                <div class="card">\n                    <div class="card-title">2. Callback-Driven Architecture</div>\n                    <div class="card-content">\n                        Agent execution feeds events through registered callbacks (status, thinking, tool_output, approval) that route to UI layers without tight coupling. Enables real-time monitoring.\n                    </div>\n                </div>\n                <div class="card">\n                    <div class="card-title">3. Async-First Design</div>\n                    <div class="card-content">\n                        All I/O operations use asyncio with non-blocking patterns. Long-running operations run in thread pools to prevent event loop blocking.\n                    </div>\n                </div>\n                <div class="card">\n                    <div class="card-title">4. Token-Aware Context Management</div>\n                    <div class="card-content">\n                        System tracks token consumption at multiple levels (message, turn, session) and implements intelligent context compaction, chunking, and message selection.\n                    </div>\n                </div>\n                <div class="card">\n                    <div class="card-title">5. Multi-Layer Memory</div>\n                    <div class="card-content">\n                        Working memory (in-turn), semantic memory (session-scoped), and deep memory (long-term archive) provide different retrieval patterns optimized for different use cases.\n                    </div>\n                </div>\n                <div class="card">\n                    <div class="card-title">6. Guard Rails & Approval Workflows</div>\n                    <div class="card-content">\n                        Input/output guards with configurable levels and tool execution approval callbacks enable safe autonomous operation with human oversight.\n                    </div>\n                </div>\n                <div class="card">\n                    <div class="card-title">7. Scale Detection & Micro-Loops</div>\n                    <div class="card-content">\n                        Automatic detection of large-scale list-processing tasks triggers specialized micro-loop that processes items one-at-a-time with constant context.\n                    </div>\n                </div>\n                <div class="card">\n                    <div class="card-title">8. Orchestration & Parallelization</div>\n                    <div class="card-content">\n                        SessionOrchestrator decomposes complex requests into DAGs, executes tasks in parallel with dependency constraints, and manages timeout/retry policies.\n                    </div>\n                </div>\n                <div class="card">\n                    <div class="card-title">9. File Registry & Cross-Task Sharing</div>\n                    <div class="card-content">\n                        FileRegistry maps logical paths to physical locations, enabling downstream tasks to discover and reference upstream artifacts.\n                    </div>\n                </div>\n                <div class="card">\n                    <div class="card-title">10. Configuration Hierarchy</div>\n                    <div class="card-content">\n                        Environment variables → .env file → config.yaml (home) → config.yaml (local) → hardcoded defaults provide flexible configuration with security overrides.\n                    </div>\n                </div>\n            </div>\n        </div>\n        \n        <!-- Technical Achievements -->\n        <div class="section">\n            <h2 class="section-title">Notable Technical Achievements</h2>\n            \n            <div class="grid-2">\n                <div class="card">\n                    <div class="card-title">Token-Efficient Browser Automation</div>\n                    <div class="card-content">\n                        PinchTab uses accessibility trees (~800 tokens) instead of screenshots (~2K+ tokens), achieving 2-3x token efficiency for web automation while maintaining semantic understanding.\n                    </div>\n                </div>\n                <div class="card">\n                    <div class="card-title">Chunked Processing Pipeline</div>\n                    <div class="card-content">\n                        Automatically detects context overflow and splits large documents into chunks, processes independently, and combines results via LLM synthesis without losing coherence.\n                    </div>\n                </div>\n                <div class="card">\n                    <div class="card-title">Dual-Mode Orchestration</div>\n                    <div class="card-content">\n                        Supports both fast "loop" mode (direct tool execution) and "contracts" mode (planner + critic validation) for different task complexity levels and performance requirements.\n                    </div>\n                </div>\n                <div class="card">\n                    <div class="card-title">Intelligent Scale Detection</div>\n                    <div class="card-content">\n                        Automatically detects large-scale tasks and switches to per-item processing to prevent context explosion, with automatic list extraction after content fetch.\n                    </div>\n                </div>\n                <div class="card">\n                    <div class="card-title">Multi-Provider LLM Abstraction</div>\n                    <div class="card-content">\n                        Unified interface supporting Ollama, OpenAI, Anthropic, Gemini, xAI with provider-specific quirks (Anthropic caching, Gemini streaming) handled transparently.\n                    </div>\n                </div>\n                <div class="card">\n                    <div class="card-title">Hybrid Memory Search</div>\n                    <div class="card-content">\n                        Combines full-text search (BM25) with vector embeddings and temporal decay scoring for intelligent context retrieval across multiple timescales and relevance dimensions.\n                    </div>\n                </div>\n                <div class="card">\n                    <div class="card-title">Graceful Degradation</div>\n                    <div class="card-content">\n                        Every failure point has a fallback (chunk LLM failure → skip chunk; combine overflow → concatenate; vision failure → return path). System remains operational with reduced capabilities.\n                    </div>\n                </div>\n                <div class="card">\n                    <div class="card-title">Comprehensive Logging & Observability</div>\n                    <div class="card-content">\n                        structlog-based structured logging with dynamic sink routing. Enables real-time monitoring, debugging, and performance analysis across distributed components.\n                    </div>\n                </div>\n            </div>\n        </div>\n        \n        <!-- Configuration & Utilities -->\n        <div class="section">\n            <h2 class="section-title">Configuration & Utilities</h2>\n            \n            <div class="grid-3">\n                <div class="card">\n                    <div class="card-title">Configuration System</div>\n                    <div class="card-content">\n                        Pydantic v2 with nested models. YAML persistence with local/home precedence. Environment variable overrides for secrets. Supports 30+ subsystems.\n                    </div>\n                </div>\n                <div class="card">\n                    <div class="card-title">Cron System</div>\n                    <div class="card-content">\n                        Human-readable schedule parsing (interval, daily, weekly). Job execution with trigger tracking. History persistence for audit and debugging.\n                    </div>\n                </div>\n                <div class="card">\n                    <div class="card-title">Instruction Management</div>\n                    <div class="card-content">\n                        Two-tier directory system (system defaults + personal overrides). Markdown template rendering with partial substitution and micro-template variants.\n                    </div>\n                </div>\n                <div class="card">\n                    <div class="card-title">Personality System</div>\n                    <div class="card-content">\n                        Agent and per-user personality profiles. Markdown-based configuration. Prompt block injection for context-specific behavior customization.\n                    </div>\n                </div>\n                <div class="card">\n                    <div class="card-title">Visualization Styles</div>\n                    <div class="card-content">\n                        Design preference management. LLM-powered style extraction from images/documents. Cache invalidation on updates for consistent rendering.\n                    </div>\n                </div>\n                <div class="card">\n                    <div class="card-title">Datastore</div>\n                    <div class="card-content">\n                        SQLite-backed relational database. Multi-format import/export (CSV, XLSX, JSON). Granular protection system (table/column/row/cell level).\n                    </div>\n                </div>\n                <div class="card">\n                    <div class="card-title">Orchestration</div>\n                    <div class="card-content">\n                        DAG-based task decomposition and execution. Parallel task activation with traffic-light gating. Timeout management with warning/grace/restart flow.\n                    </div>\n                </div>\n                <div class="card">\n                    <div class="card-title">Skills System</div>\n                    <div class="card-content">\n                        Skill discovery from multiple sources. GitHub-based installation. Dependency management (brew, npm, go, uv). LLM-based skill ranking.\n                    </div>\n                </div>\n                <div class="card">\n                    <div class="card-title">Session Management</div>\n                    <div class="card-content">\n                        SQLite-backed persistence for conversations, tasks, contacts, scripts, APIs, playbooks, workflows, credentials. Cross-session state management via app_state table.\n                    </div>\n                </div>\n            </div>\n        </div>\n        \n        <!-- File Organization -->\n        <div class="section">\n            <h2 class="section-title">File Organization</h2>\n            \n            <div class="code-block">\ncaptain_claw/\n├── Core Agent Engine (13 files)\n│   ├── agent.py (main class)\n│   ├── agent_*_mixin.py (13 specialized mixins)\n│   └── agent_pool.py (worker management)\n│\n├── Tools Ecosystem (40+ files)\n│   ├── tools/\n│   │   ├── browser.py, pinchtab.py (web automation)\n│   │   ├── web_fetch.py, web_search.py (web tools)\n│   │   ├── google_*.py (Google Workspace)\n│   │   ├── read.py, write.py, edit.py, glob.py (file ops)\n│   │   ├── datastore.py, typesense.py (data)\n│   │   ├── document_extract.py (document processing)\n│   │   ├── shell.py, desktop_action.py (system)\n│   │   ├── todo.py, contacts.py, playbooks.py (productivity)\n│   │   └── ... (30+ more tools)\n│\n├── Web Infrastructure (30+ files)\n│   ├── web/\n│   │   ├── web_server.py (main server)\n│   │   ├── ws_handler.py, chat_handler.py (WebSocket)\n│   │   ├── rest_*.py (50+ REST endpoints)\n│   │   ├── static_pages.py (23 HTML templates)\n│   │   └── ... <li><strong>browser_network.py</strong> — Network traffic interception</li>\n                    </ul>\n                </div>\n                \n                <div class="card">\n              <li><strong>desktop_action.py</strong> — GUI automation (mouse, keyboard)</li>\n                        <li><strong>screen_capture.py</strong> — Screenshot capture</li>\n                        <li><strong>clipboard.py</strong> — macOS clipboard operations</li>\n                        <li><strong>termux.py</strong> — Android device control</li>\n <div class="section">\n            <h2 class="section-title">Memory Architecture</h2>\n            \n            <div class="grid-2">\n                <div class="card">\n                    <div class="card-title">Working Memory</div>\n                    <div class="card-content">\n                        In-turn context buffer with automatic compaction. Holds current conversation state and tool results within the LLM\'s context window. Implements sliding-window compression when token limits are approached.\n                    </div>\n                </div>\n                <div class="card">\n                    <div class="card-title">Semantic Memory</div>\n                    <div class="card-content">\n                        Session-scoped SQLite FTS5 + vector embeddings with hybrid search. Combines full-text search (BM25) with vector similarity and temporal decay scoring for intelligent context retrieval.\n                    </div>\n                </div>\n                <div class="card">\n                    <div class="card-title">Deep Memory</div>\n                    <div class="card-content">\n                        Typesense-backed long-term archive with chunking and embedding. Stores historical data across sessions for cross-session learning and reference.\n                    </div>\n                </div>\n                <div class="card">\n                    <div class="card-title">File Registry</div>\n                    <div class="card-content">\n                        Logical-to-physical path mapping for cross-task artifact discovery. Enables downstream tasks to reference upstream artifacts without knowledge of session IDs or directory structures.\n                    </div>\n                </div>\n            </div>\n        </div>\n        \n        <!-- LLM Provider Support -->\n        <div class="section">\n            <h2 class="section-title">Multi-Provider LLM Support</h2>\n            \n            <div client for local models</li>\n                    </ul>\n                </div>\n                <div class="card">\n                    <div class="card-title">Advanced Features</div>\n                    <ul class="feature-list">\n                        <li>Token rate limiting with sliding-window backpressure</li>\n                        <li>Provider-specific message/tool conversion</li>\n                        <li>Unified tool definition schema</li>\n                        <li>Streaming response collection</li>\n                        <li>Token counting and usage tracking</li>\n                    </ul>\n                </div>\n            </div>\n        </div>\n        \n        <!-- Web Infrastructure -->\n        <div class="section">\n            <h2 class="section-title">Web <div class="card-title">aiohttp Web Server</div>\n                    <div class="card-content">\n                        Async web server with 100+ HTTP/WebSocket route handlers. Real-time callback routing to connected clients without tight coupling. Multi-session state management and third-party integration orchestration.\n                    </div>\n                </div>\n                <div class="card">\n                    <div class="card-title">WebSocket Communication</div>\n                    <div class="card-content">\n                        Real-time bidirectional communication for chat messages, session state sync, and live speech-to-text streaming. User approval workflow with pairing tokens. Typing indicators and inline keyboards for next steps. Image upload/download support and slash command execution.\n                    </div>\n                </div>\n                <div class="card">\n                    <div class="card-title">Discord Bridge</div>\n                    <div class="card-content">\n                        DM-based polling interface with message normalization. Bot mention detection and audio file upload support. Lightweight integration for Discord communities.\n                    </div>\n                </div>\n                <div class="card">\n                    <div class="card-title">Slack Bridge</div>\n                    <div class="card-content">\n                        DM-first polling with pagination support. User caching and username resolution. Thread reply support for organized conversations.\n                    </div>\n                </div>\n                <div class="card">\n                    <div class="card-title">Google Workspace</div>\n                    <div class="card-content">\n                        PKCE-based OAuth authorization flow. Token lifecycle management and credential injection. Full integration with Drive, Docs, Sheets, Calendar, and Gmail.\n                    </div>\n                </div>\n            </div>\n        </div>\n        \n        <!-- Tool Distribution Chart -->\n        <div class="section">\n            <h2 class="section-title">Tool Distribution by Category</h2>\n            <div class="chart-container">\n                <canvas id="toolDistributionChart"></canvas>\n            </div>\n        </div>\n        \n        <!-- Key Design Patterns -->\n        <div class="section">\n            <h2 class="section-title">Key Design Patterns</h2>\n            \n            <div class="grid-2">\n                <div class="card">\n                    <div class="card-title">1. Mixin-Based Composition</div>\n                    <div class="card-content">\n                        The Agent class uses 13 mixins to provide distinct capabilities without deep inheritance hierarchies. Each mixin focuses on a specific concern, enabling modular testing and feature toggling.\n                    </div>\n                </div>\n                <div class="card">\n                    <div class="card-title">2. Callback-Driven Architecture</div>\n                    <div class="card-content">\n                        Agent execution feeds events through registered callbacks (status, thinking, tool_output, approval) that route to UI layers without tight coupling. Enables real-time monitoring.\n                    </div>\n                </div>\n                <div class="card">\n                    <div class="card-title">3. Async-First Design</div>\n                    <div class="card-content">\n                        All I/O operations use asyncio with non-blocking patterns. Long-running operations run in thread pools to prevent event loop blocking.\n                    </div>\n                </div>\n                <div class="card">\n                    <div class="card-title">4. Token-Aware Context Management</div>\n                    <div class="card-content">\n                        System tracks token consumption at multiple levels (message, turn, session) and implements intelligent context compaction, chunking, and message selection.\n                    </div>\n                </div>\n                <div class="card">\n                    <div class="card-title">5. Multi-Layer Memory</div>\n                    <div class="card-content">\n                        Working memory (in-turn), semantic memory (session-scoped), and deep memory (long-term archive) provide different retrieval patterns optimized for different use cases.\n                    </div>\n                </div>\n                <div class="card">\n                    <div class="card-title">6. Guard Rails & Approval Workflows</div>\n                    <div class="card-content">\n                        Input/output guards with configurable levels and tool execution approval callbacks enable safe autonomous operation with human oversight.\n                    </div>\n                </div>\n                <div class="card">\n                    <div class="card-title">7. Scale Detection & Micro-Loops</div>\n                    <div class="card-content">\n                        Automatic detection of large-scale list-processing tasks triggers specialized micro-loop that processes items one-at-a-time with constant context.\n                    </div>\n                </div>\n                <div class="card">\n                    <div class="card-title">8. Orchestration & Parallelization</div>\n                    <div class="card-content">\n                        SessionOrchestrator decomposes complex requests into DAGs, executes tasks in parallel with dependency constraints, and manages timeout/retry policies.\n                    </div>\n                </div>\n                <div class="card">\n                    <div class="card-title">9. File Registry & Cross-Task Sharing</div>\n                    <div class="card-content">\n                        FileRegistry maps logical paths to physical locations, enabling downstream tasks to discover and reference upstream artifacts.\n                    </div>\n                </div>\n                <div class="card">\n                    <div class="card-title">10. Configuration Hierarchy</div>\n                    <div class="card-content">\n                        Environment variables → .env file → config.yaml (home) → config.yaml (local) → hardcoded defaults provide flexible configuration with security overrides.\n                    </div>\n                </div>\n            </div>\n        </div>\n        \n        <!-- Technical Achievements -->\n        <div class="section">\n            <h2 class="section-title">Notable Technical Achievements</h2>\n            \n            <div class="grid-2">\n                <div class="card">\n                    <div class="card-title">Token-Efficient Browser Automation</div>\n                    <div class="card-content">\n                        PinchTab uses accessibility trees (~800 tokens) instead of screenshots (~2K+ tokens), achieving 2-3x token efficiency for web automation while maintaining semantic understanding.\n                    </div>\n                </div>\n                <div class="card">\n                    <div class="card-title">Chunked Processing Pipeline</div>\n                    <div class="card-content">\n                        Automatically detects context overflow and splits large documents into chunks, processes independently, and combines results via LLM synthesis without losing coherence.\n                    </div>\n                </div>\n                <div class="card">\n                    <div class="card-title">Dual-Mode Orchestration</div>\n                    <div class="card-content">\n                        Supports both fast "loop" mode (direct tool execution) and "contracts" mode (planner + critic validation) for different task complexity levels and performance requirements.\n                    </div>\n                </div>\n                <div class="card">\n                    <div class="card-title">Intelligent Scale Detection</div>\n                    <div class="card-content">\n                        Automatically detects large-scale tasks and switches to per-item processing to prevent context explosion, with automatic list extraction after content fetch.\n                    </div>\n                </div>\n                <div class="card">\n                    <div class="card-title">Multi-Provider LLM Abstraction</div>\n                    <div class="card-content">\n                        Unified </div>\n                <div class="card">\n                    <div class="card-title">Hybrid Memory Search</div>\n                    <div class="card-content">\n                        Combines full-text search (BM25) with vector embeddings and temporal decay scoring for intelligent context retrieval across multiple timescales and relevance dimensions.\n                    </div>\n                </div>\n                <div class="card">\n                    <div class="card-title">Graceful Degradation</div>\n                    <div class="card-content">\n                        Every failure point has a fallback (chunk LLM failure → skip chunk; combine overflow → concatenate; vision failure → return path). System remains operational with reduced capabilities.\n                    </div>\n                </div>\n                <div class="card">\n                    <div class="card-title">Comprehensive Logging & Observability</div>\n                    <div class="card-content">\n                        structlog-based structured logging with dynamic sink routing. </div>\n\n        <!-- Design Patterns -->\n        <div class="section">\n            <div class="section-title">Key Design Patterns</div>\n\n            <div class="design-pattern">\n                <h4>1. Mixin-Based Composition</h4>\n                <p>The Agent class uses 13 mixins to provide distinct capabilities without deep inheritance hierarchies. Each mixin focuses on a specific concern (orchestration, tools, context, memory, etc.), enabling modular testing and feature toggling.</p>\n            </div>\n\n            <div class="design-pattern">\n                <h4>2. Callback-Driven Architecture</h4>\n                <p>Agent execution feeds events through registered callbacks (status, thinking, tool_output, approval) that route to UI layers without tight coupling. Enables real-time monitoring and multi-client synchronization.</p>\n            </div>\n\n            <div class="design-pattern">\n                <h4>3. Async-First Design</h4>\n                <p>All I/O operations use asyncio with non-blocking patterns. Long-running operations (LLM calls, file I/O, network requests) run in thread pools to prevent event loop blocking.</p>\n            </div>\n\n            <div class="design-pattern">\n                <h4>4. Token-Aware Context Management</h4>\n                <p>The system tracks token consumption at multiple levels (message, turn, session) and implements intelligent context compaction, chunking, and message selection to stay within LLM context windows.</p>\n            </div>\n\n            <div class="design-pattern">\n                <h4>5. Multi-Layer Memory</h4>\n                <p>Working memory (in-turn), semantic memory (session-scoped), and deep memory (long-term archive) provide different retrieval patterns optimized for recency, relevance, and scale.</p>\n            </div>\n\n            <div class="design-pattern">\n                <h4>6. Guard Rails & Approval Workflows</h4>\n                <p>Input/output guards with configurable levels (stop_suspicious, ask_for_approval) and tool execution approval callbacks enable safe autonomous operation with human oversight.</p>\n            </div>\n\n            <div class="design-pattern">\n                <h4>7. Scale Detection & Micro-Loops</h4>\n                <p>Automatic detection of large-scale list-processing tasks triggers a specialized micro-loop that processes items one-at-a-time with constant context, preventing context window overflow.</p>\n            </div>\n\n            <div class="design-pattern">\n                <h4>8. Orchestration & Parallelization</h4>\n                <p>SessionOrchestrator decomposes complex requests into DAGs, executes tasks in parallel with dependency constraints, and manages timeout/retry policies for resilient multi-step workflows.</p>\n            </div>\n\n            <div class="design-pattern">\n                <h4>9. File Registry & Cross-Task Sharing</h4>\n                <p>FileRegistry maps logical paths to physical locations, enabling downstream tasks to discover and reference upstream artifacts without knowledge of session IDs or directory structures.</p>\n            </div>\n\n            <div class="design-pattern">\n                <h4>10. Configuration Hierarchy</h4>\n                <p>Environment variables → .env file → config.yaml (home) → config.yaml (local) → hardcoded defaults provide flexible configuration with security-sensitive overrides.</p>\n            </div>\n        </div>\n\n        <!-- Technical Achievements -->\n        <div class="section">\n            <div class="section-title">Notable Technical Achievements</div>\n\n            <div class="achievement">\n                <strong>🎯 Token-Efficient Browser Automation</strong>\n                <p>PinchTab uses accessibility trees (~800 tokens) instead of screenshots (~2K+ tokens), achieving 2-3x token efficiency for web automation tasks.</p>\n            </div>\n\n            <div class="achievement">\n                <strong>📚 Chunked Processing Pipeline</strong>\n                <p>Automatically detects context overflow and splits large documents into chunks, processes independently, and combines results via LLM class="card">\n                    <h3>Working Memory</h3>\n                    <p><strong>In-turn context buffer</strong> with automatic compaction. Holds current conversation state and recent messages for immediate context.</p>\n                </div>\n                <div class="card">\n                    <h3>Semantic Memory</h3>\n                    <p><strong>SQLite FTS5 + vector embeddings</strong> with hybrid search. Session-scoped retrieval optimized for relevance and recency.</p>\n                </div>\n                <div class="card">\n                    <h3>Deep Memory</h3>\n                    <p><strong>Typesense-backed long-term archive</strong> with chunking and embedding. Persistent storage across sessions with vector similarity search.</p>\n                </div>\n                <div class="card">\n                    <h3>File Registry</h3>\n                    <p><strong>Logical-to-physical path mapping</strong> for cross-task artifact discovery. Enables downstream tasks to reference upstream outputs.</p>\n                </div>\n            </div>\n        </div>\n\n        <!-- Web Infrastructure -->\n        <div class="section">\n            <div class="section-title">Web UI Infrastructure</div>\n            \n            <div class="chart-container">\n                <div class="chart-title">API Endpoints Distribution</div>\n                <canvas id="apiChart"></canvas>\n            </div>\n\n            <div class="grid-2">\n                <div class="card">\n                    <h3>Core Server</h3>\n                    <p>aiohttp-based async web server with 100+ HTTP/WebSocket routes.       <div class="chart-title">Supported Integration Platforms</div>\n                <canvas id="platformChart"></canvas>\n            </div>\n\n            <div class="grid-2">\n                <div slash commands, and cron job management.</p>\n                </div>\n                <div class="architecture-box">\n                    <h4>Discord</h4>\n                    <p>DM-based polling interface with message normalization, bot mention detection, and audio file upload support.</p>\n                </div>\n                <div class="architecture-box">\n                    <h4>Slack</h4>\n                    <p>DM-first polling with pagination, user caching, username resolution, and thread reply support.</p>\n                </div>\n                <div provider.</p>\n                </div>\n                <div class="architecture-box">\n                    <h4>BotPort Network</h4>\n                    <p>Distributed agent coordination with concern-based task delegation and multi-hop agent communication.</p>\n                </div>\n                <div class="architecture-box">\n                    <h4>Hotkey Daemon</h4>\n                    <p>Global keyboard listener for voice activation with double/triple-tap state machine, screenshot capture, and clipboard detection.</p>\n                </div>\n            </div>\n        </div>\n\n        <!-- Design Patterns -->\n        <div class="section">\n            <div class="section-title">Key Design Patterns</div>\n\n            <div class="design-pattern">\n                <h4>1. Mixin-Based Composition</h4>\n                <p>The Agent class uses 13 mixins to provide distinct capabilities without deep inheritance hierarchies. Each mixin focuses on a specific concern (orchestration, tools, context, memory, etc.), enabling modular testing and feature toggling.</p>\n            </div>\n\n            <div class="design-pattern">\n                <h4>2. Callback-Driven Architecture</h4>\n                <p>Agent execution feeds events through registered callbacks (status, thinking, tool_output, approval) that route to UI layers without tight coupling. Enables real-time monitoring and multi-client synchronization.</p>\n            </div>\n\n            <div class="design-pattern">\n                <h4>3. Async-First Design</h4>\n                <p>All I/O operations use asyncio with non-blocking patterns. Long-running operations (LLM calls, file I/O, network requests) run in thread pools to prevent event loop blocking.</p>\n            </div>\n\n            <div class="design-pattern">\n                <h4>4. Token-Aware Context Management</h4>\n                <p>The system tracks token consumption at multiple levels (message, turn, session) and implements intelligent context compaction, chunking, and message selection to stay within LLM context windows.</p>\n            </div>\n\n            <div class="design-pattern">\n                <h4>5. Multi-Layer Memory</h4>\n                <p>Working memory (in-turn), semantic memory (session-scoped), and deep memory (long-term archive) provide different retrieval patterns optimized for recency, relevance, and scale.</p>\n            </div>\n\n            <div class="design-pattern">\n                <h4>6. Guard Rails & Approval Workflows</h4>\n                <p>Input/output guards with configurable levels (stop_suspicious, ask_for_approval) and tool execution approval callbacks enable safe autonomous operation with human oversight.</p>\n            </div>\n\n            <div class="design-pattern">\n                <h4>7. Scale Detection & Micro-Loops</h4>\n                <p>Automatic detection of large-scale list-processing tasks triggers a specialized micro-loop that processes items one-at-a-time with constant context, preventing context window overflow.</p>\n            </div>\n\n            <div class="design-pattern">\n                <h4>8. Orchestration & Parallelization</h4>\n                <p>SessionOrchestrator decomposes complex requests into DAGs, executes tasks in parallel with dependency constraints, and manages timeout/retry policies for resilient multi-step workflows.</p>\n            </div>\n\n            <div class="design-pattern">\n                <h4>9. File Registry & Cross-Task Sharing</h4>\n                <p>FileRegistry maps logical paths to physical locations, enabling downstream tasks to discover and reference upstream artifacts without knowledge of session IDs or directory structures.</p>\n            </div>\n\n            <div class="design-pattern">\n                <h4>10. Configuration Hierarchy</h4>\n                <p>Environment variables → .env file → config.yaml (home) → config.yaml (local) → hardcoded defaults provide flexible configuration with security-sensitive overrides.</p>\n            </div>\n        </div>\n\n        <!-- Technical Achievements -->\n        <div class="section">\n            <div class="section-title">Notable Technical Achievements</div>\n\n            <div class="achievement">\n                <strong>🎯 Token-Efficient Browser Automation</strong>\n                <p>PinchTab uses accessibility trees (~800 tokens) instead of screenshots (~2K+ tokens), achieving 2-3x token efficiency for web automation tasks.</p>\n            </div>\n\n            <div class="achievement">\n                <strong>📚 Chunked Processing Pipeline</strong>\n                <p>Automatically detects context overflow and splits large documents into chunks, processes independently, and combines results via LLM synthesis.</p>\n            </div>\n\n            <div class="achievement">\n                <strong>🔀 Dual-Mode Orchestration</strong>\n                <p>Supports both fast "loop" mode (direct tool execution) and "contracts" mode (planner + critic validation) for different task complexity levels.</p>\n            </div>\n\n            <div class="achievement">\n                <strong>📊 Intelligent Scale Detection</strong>\n                <p>Automatically detects large-scale tasks and switches to per-item processing to prevent context explosion, with automatic list extraction after content fetch.</p>\n            </div>\n\n            <div class="achievement">\n                <strong>🔌 Multi-Provider LLM Abstraction</strong>\n                <p>Unified interface supporting Ollama, OpenAI, Anthropic, Gemini, xAI with provider-specific quirks handled transparently.</p>\n            </div>\n\n            <div class="achievement">\n                <strong>🧠 Hybrid Memory Search</strong>\n                <p>Combines full-text search (BM25) with vector embeddings and temporal decay scoring for intelligent context retrieval across multiple timescales.</p>\n            </div>\n\n            <div class="achievement">\n                <strong>⚡ Graceful Degradation</strong>\n                <p>Every failure point has a fallback (chunk LLM failure → skip chunk; combine overflow → concatenate; vision failure → return screenshot path).</p>\n            </div>\n        </div>\n\n        <!-- LLM Providers -->\n        <div class="section">\n            <div MEMORY (memory.py)                             │\n│  • In-turn context buffer                               │\n│  • Automatic compaction on overflow                     │\n│  • Recency-weighted retrieval                           │\n│  • Token-aware message selection                        │\n└─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┘\n │\n└─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┘\n```\n\n### Session Persistence (session.py)\n- SQLite-backed storage for conversations, tasks, contacts, scripts, APIs, playbooks, dependency tracking\n\n---\n\n## 🔄 AGENT EXECUTION FLOW\n\n### Main Orchestration Loop (agent_orchestration_mixin.py)\n\n```\n1. RECEIVE REQUEST\n   └─ Parse user input & extract parameters\n\n2. CONTEXT BUILDING (agent_context_mixin.py)\n   ├─ Retrieve semantic memory matches\n   ├─ Construct dynamic system prompt\n   ├─ Select messages within token budget\n   └─ Prepare LLM input\n\n3. LLM INVOCATION\n   ├─ Call LLM provider (Ollama/OpenAI/Claude/Gemini/Grok)\n   ├─ Handle streaming responses\n   ├─ Extract tool calls via JSON parsing\n   └─ Track token consumption\n\n4. TOOL EXECUTION (agent_tool_loop_mixin.py)\n   ├─ Validate tool calls (duplicate detection, scale guards)\n   ├─ Execute tools in parallel where possible\n   ├─ Collect results with error handling\n   ├─ Append results to message history\n   └─ Detect scale-related tasks → trigger micro-loop\n\n5. COMPLETION VALIDATION (agent_completion_mixin.py)\n   ├─ Multi-stage validation gates\n   ├─ Check task requirements met\n   ├─ Verify response quality\n   └─ Gate response finalization\n\n6. RESPONSE DELIVERY\n   ├─ Format response for client\n   ├─ Send via callbacks (status, thinking, tool_output)\n   ├─ Persist to session database\n   └─ Update semantic memory\n\n7. ITERATION MANAGEMENT\n   ├─ Check iteration budget (prevent infinite loops)\n   ├─ Decide: continue loop or finalize\n   └─ Handle timeouts & early termination\n```\n\n---\n\n## 📊 KEY DESIGN PATTERNS\n\n### 1. Mixin-Based Composition\nThe Agent class uses 13 specialized mixins to provide distinct capabilities without deep inheritance hierarchies. Each mixin focuses on a specific concern, enabling modular testing and feature toggling.\n\n**Benefit:** Clean separation of concerns, easy to test individual mixins, simple to add new capabilities.\n\n### 2. Callback-Driven Architecture\nAgent execution feeds events through registered callbacks (status, thinking, tool_output, approval) that route to UI layers without tight coupling.\n\n**Benefit:** Real-time monitoring, multi-client synchronization, extensible event system.\n\n### 3. Async-First Design\nAll I/O operations use asyncio with non-blocking patterns. Long-running operations (LLM calls, file I/O, network requests) run in thread pools.\n\n**Benefit:** High concurrency, responsive UI, efficient resource utilization.\n\n### 4. Token-Aware Context Management\nThe system tracks token consumption at multiple levels (message, turn, session) and implements intelligent context compaction, chunking, and message selection.\n\n**Benefit:** Prevents context window overflow, optimizes LLM costs, maintains coherent context.\n\n### 5. Multi-Layer Memory\nWorking memory (in-turn), semantic memory (session-scoped), and deep memory (long-term archive) provide different retrieval patterns optimized for recency, relevance, and scale.\n\n**Benefit:** Efficient context retrieval, scalable to long conversations, intelligent knowledge management.\n\n### 6. Guard Rails & Approval Workflows\nInput/output guards with configurable levels (stop_suspicious, ask_for_approval) and tool execution approval callbacks enable safe autonomous operation.\n\n**Benefit:** Human oversight, content safety, compliance with policies.\n\n### 7. Scale Detection & Micro-Loops\nAutomatic detection of large-scale list-processing tasks triggers a specialized micro-loop that processes items one-at-a-time with constant context.\n\n**Benefit:** Prevents context explosion, handles 100+ item batches, maintains consistent token usage.\n\n### 8. Orchestration & Parallelization\nSessionOrchestrator decomposes complex requests into DAGs, executes tasks in parallel with dependency constraints, and manages timeout/retry policies.\n\n**Benefit:** Faster execution, resilient workflows, intelligent task decomposition.\n\n### 9. File Registry & Cross-Task Sharing\nFileRegistry maps logical paths to physical locations, enabling downstream tasks to discover and reference upstream artifacts.\n\n**Benefit:** Seamless artifact sharing, reduced manual path management, cross-task dependencies.\n\n### 10. Configuration Hierarchy\nEnvironment variables → .env file → config.yaml (home) → config.yaml (local) → hardcoded defaults.\n\n**Benefit:** Flexible configuration, security-sensitive overrides, environment-specific settings.\n\n---\n\n## 🎯 NOTABLE TECHNICAL ACHIEVEMENTS\n\n### 1. Token-Efficient Browser Automation\n**PinchTab** uses accessibility trees (~800 tokens) instead of screenshots (~2K+ tokens), achieving **2-3x token efficiency** for web automation.\n\n### 2. Chunked Processing Pipeline\nAutomatically detects context overflow and splits large documents into chunks, processes independently, and combines results via LLM synthesis.\n\n### 3. Dual-Mode Orchestration\nSupports both fast "loop" mode (direct tool execution) and "contracts" mode (planner + critic validation) for different task complexity levels.\n\n### 4. Intelligent Scale Detection\nAutomatically detects large-scale tasks and switches to per-item processing to prevent context explosion, with automatic list extraction after content fetch.\n\n### 5. Multi-Provider LLM Abstraction\nUnified interface supporting Ollama, OpenAI, Anthropic, Gemini, xAI with provider-specific quirks handled transparently.\n\n### 6. Hybrid Memory Search\nCombines full-text search (BM25) with vector embeddings and temporal decay scoring for intelligent context retrieval.\n\n### 7. Graceful Degradation\nEvery failure point has a fallback (chunk LLM failure → skip chunk; combine overflow → concatenate; vision failure → return screenshot path).\n\n### 8. Distributed Agent Coordination\nBotPort network enables multi-hop agent communication and concern-based task delegation across agent instances.\n\n### 9. Real-Time Streaming\nWebSocket-based streaming with callback routing enables real-time status updates, thinking visibility, and multi-client synchronization.\n\n### 10. Encrypted Credential Management\nBrowser credentials stored encrypted in SQLite with provider-specific auth patterns (OAuth, API keys, basic auth, cookies).\n\n---\n\n## 📈 SYSTEM STATISTICS\n\n| skill discovery and installation\n\n---\n\n## 🧠 MEMORY & PERSISTENCE ARCHITECTURE\n\n### Three-Layer Memory System\n\n```\n┌─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┐\n│  WORKING MEMORY (memory.py)                             │\n│  • In-turn context buffer                               │\n│  • Automatic compaction on overflow                     │\n│  • Recency-weighted retrieval                           │\n│  • Token-aware message selection                        │\n└─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┘\n                          ↓\n┌─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┐\n│  SEMANTIC MEMORY (semantic_memory.py)                   │\n│  • SQLite FTS5 full-text search                         │\n│  • Vector embeddings for similarity                     │\n│  • Hybrid keyword + vector search                       │\n│  • Session-scoped persistence                          │\n│  • Temporal decay scoring                               │\n└─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┘\n                          ↓\n┌─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┐\n│  DEEP MEMORY (deep_memory.py)                           │\n│  • Typesense long-term archive                          │\n│  • Document chunking & embedding                        │\n│  • Cross-session retrieval                              │\n│  • Scalable to millions of documents                    │\n│  • Tag-based filtering                                  │\n└─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┘\n```\n\n### Session Persistence (session.py)\n- SQLite-backed storage for conversations, tasks, contacts, scripts, APIs, playbooks, workflows\n- Message history with tool call metadata and token counting\n- Cron job scheduling with execution history\n- Cross-session state management via app_state table\n\n### File Registry (file_registry.py)\n- Logical-to-physical path mapping for artifact discovery\n- Enables downstream tasks to reference upstream outputs without session ID knowledge\n- Cross-task file sharing and dependency tracking\n\n---\n\n## 🔄 AGENT EXECUTION FLOW\n\n### Main Orchestration Loop (agent_orchestration_mixin.py)\n\n```\n1. RECEIVE REQUEST\n   └─ Parse user input & extract parameters\n\n2. CONTEXT BUILDING (agent_context_mixin.py)\n   ├─ Retrieve semantic memory matches\n   ├─ Construct dynamic system prompt\n   ├─ Select messages within token budget\n   └─ Prepare LLM input\n\n3. LLM INVOCATION\n   ├─ Call LLM provider (Ollama/OpenAI/Claude/Gemini/Grok)\n   ├─ Handle streaming responses\n   ├─ Extract tool calls via JSON parsing\n   └─ Track token consumption\n\n4. TOOL EXECUTION (agent_tool_loop_mixin.py)\n   ├─ Validate tool calls (duplicate detection, scale guards)\n   ├─ Execute tools in parallel where possible\n   ├─ Collect results with error handling\n   ├─ Append results to message history\n   └─ Detect scale-related tasks → trigger micro-loop\n\n5. COMPLETION VALIDATION (agent_completion_mixin.py)\n   ├─ Multi-stage validation gates\n   ├─ Check task requirements met\n   ├─ Verify response quality\n   └─ Gate response finalization\n\n6. RESPONSE DELIVERY\n   ├─ Format response for client\n   ├─ Send via callbacks (status, thinking, tool_output)\n   ├─ Persist to session database\n   └─ Update semantic memory\n\n7. ITERATION MANAGEMENT\n   ├─ Check iteration budget (prevent infinite loops)\n   ├─ Decide: continue loop or finalize\n   └─ Handle timeouts & early termination\n```\n\n---\n\n## 📊 KEY DESIGN PATTERNS\n\n### 1. Mixin-Based Composition\nThe Agent class uses 13 specialized mixins to provide distinct capabilities without deep inheritance hierarchies. Each mixin focuses on a specific concern, enabling modular testing and feature toggling.\n\n**Benefit:** Clean separation of concerns, easy to test individual mixins, simple to add new capabilities.\n\n### 2. Callback-Driven Architecture\nAgent execution feeds events through registered callbacks (status, thinking, tool_output, approval) that route to UI layers without tight coupling.\n\n**Benefit:** Real-time monitoring, multi-client synchronization, extensible event system.\n\n### 3. Async-First Design\nAll I/O operations use asyncio with non-blocking patterns. Long-running operations (LLM calls, file I/O, network requests) run in thread pools.\n\n**Benefit:** High concurrency, responsive UI, efficient resource utilization.\n\n### 4. Token-Aware Context Management\nThe system tracks token consumption at multiple levels (message, turn, session) and implements intelligent context compaction, chunking, and message selection.\n\n**Benefit:** Prevents context window overflow, optimizes LLM costs, maintains coherent context.\n\n### 5. Multi-Layer Memory\nWorking memory (in-turn), semantic memory (session-scoped), and deep memory (long-term archive) provide different retrieval patterns optimized for recency, relevance, and scale.\n\n**Benefit:** Efficient context retrieval, scalable to long conversations, intelligent knowledge management.\n\n### 6. Guard Rails & Approval Workflows\nInput/output guards with configurable levels (stop_suspicious, ask_for_approval) and tool execution approval callbacks enable safe autonomous operation.\n\n**Benefit:** Human oversight, content safety, compliance with policies.\n\n### 7. Scale Detection & Micro-Loops\nAutomatic detection of large-scale list-processing tasks triggers a specialized micro-loop that processes items one-at-a-time with constant context.\n\n**Benefit:** Prevents context explosion, handles 100+ item batches, maintains consistent token usage.\n\n### 8. Orchestration & Parallelization\nSessionOrchestrator decomposes complex requests into DAGs, executes tasks in parallel with dependency constraints, and manages timeout/retry policies.\n\n**Benefit:** Faster execution, resilient workflows, intelligent task decomposition.\n\n### 9. File Registry & Cross-Task Sharing\nFileRegistry maps logical paths to physical locations, enabling downstream tasks to discover and reference upstream artifacts.\n\n**Benefit:** Seamless artifact sharing, reduced manual path management, cross-task dependencies.\n\n### 10. Configuration Hierarchy\nEnvironment variables → .env file → config.yaml (home) → config.yaml (local) → hardcoded defaults.\n\n**Benefit:** Flexible configuration, security-sensitive overrides, environment-specific settings.\n\n---\n\n## 🎯 NOTABLE TECHNICAL ACHIEVEMENTS\n\n### 1. Token-Efficient Browser Automation\n**PinchTab** uses accessibility trees (~800 tokens) instead of screenshots (~2K+ tokens), achieving **2-3x token efficiency** for web automation.\n\n### 2. Chunked Processing Pipeline\nAutomatically detects context overflow and splits large documents into chunks, processes independently, and combines results via LLM synthesis.\n\n### 3. Dual-Mode Orchestration\nSupports both fast "loop" mode (direct tool execution) and "contracts" mode (planner + critic validation) for different task complexity levels.\n\n### 4. Intelligent Scale Detection\nAutomatically detects large-scale tasks and switches to per-item processing to prevent context explosion, with automatic list extraction after content fetch.\n\n### 5. Multi-Provider LLM Abstraction\nUnified interface supporting Ollama, OpenAI, Anthropic, Gemini, xAI with provider-specific quirks handled transparently.\n\n### 6. Hybrid Memory Search\nCombines full-text search (BM25) with vector embeddings and temporal decay scoring for intelligent context retrieval.\n\n### 7. Graceful Degradation\nEvery failure point has a fallback (chunk LLM failure → skip chunk; combine overflow → concatenate; vision failure → return screenshot path).\n\n### 8. Distributed Agent Coordination\nBotPort network enables multi-hop agent communication and concern-based task delegation across agent instances.\n\n### 9. Real-Time Streaming\nWebSocket-based streaming with callback routing enables real-time status updates, thinking visibility, and multi-client synchronization.\n\n### 10. Encrypted Credential Management\nBrowser credentials stored encrypted in SQLite with provider-specific auth patterns (OAuth, API keys, basic auth, cookies).\n\n---\n\n## 📈 SYSTEM STATISTICS\n\n| \n            <h3>Core Agent Engine</h3>\n            <p style="margin-bottom: 20px;">The agent system centers on a <span class="highlight">mixin-based architecture</span> where the Agent class <div class="section">\n            <h2>Key Design Patterns</h2>\n            \n            <div style="margin-bottom: 30px;">\n                <div class="arch-box">\n                    <strong>1. Mixin-Based Composition</strong> — Agent class uses 13 mixins for modular capabilities without deep inheritance hierarchies\n                </div>\n                <div class="arch-box">\n                    <strong>2. Callback-Driven Architecture</strong> — Agent execution feeds events (status, thinking, tool_output, approval) through callbacks for real-time monitoring\n                </div>\n                <div class="arch-box">\n                    <strong>3. Async-First Design</strong> — All I/O operations use asyncio with non-blocking patterns and thread pool execution\n                </div>\n                <div class="arch-box">\n                    <strong>4. Token-Aware Context Management</strong> — Multi-level token tracking with intelligent context compaction and message selection\n                </div>\n                <div class="arch-box">\n                    <strong>5. Multi-Layer Memory</strong> — Working (in-turn), Semantic (session-scoped), and Deep (long-term) memory for different retrieval patterns\n                </div>\n                <div class="arch-box">\n                    <strong>6. Guard Rails & Approval Workflows</strong> — Input/output guards with configurable levels for safe autonomous operation\n                </div>\n                <div class="arch-box">\n                    <strong>7. Scale Detection & Micro-Loops</strong> — Automatic detection of large-scale tasks triggers per-item processing with constant context\n                </div>\n                <div class="arch-box">\n                    <strong>8. Orchestration & Parallelization</strong> — DAG-based task decomposition with dependency constraints and timeout management\n                </div>\n                <div class="arch-box">\n                    <strong>9. File Registry & Cross-Task Sharing</strong> — Logical-to-physical path mapping for artifact discovery across tasks\n                </div>\n                <div class="arch-box">\n                    <strong>10. Configuration Hierarchy</strong> — Environment variables → .env → config.yaml (home) → config.yaml (local) → defaults\n                </div>\n            </div>\n        </div>\n\n        <!-- Technical Achievements -->\n        <div class="section">\n            <h2>Notable Technical Achievements</h2>\n            \n            <table>\n                <thead>\n                    <tr>\n                        <th>Achievement</th>\n                        <th>Description</th>\n                    </tr>\n                </thead>\n                <tbody>\n                    <tr>\n                        <td><strong>Token-Efficient Browser Automation</strong></td>\n                        <td>PinchTab uses accessibility trees (~800 tokens) instead of screenshots (~2K+ tokens), achieving 2-3x token efficiency</td>\n                    </tr>\n                    <tr>\n                        <td><strong>Chunked Processing Pipeline</strong></td>\n                        <td>Automatically detects context overflow and splits large documents into chunks for independent processing</td>\n                    </tr>\n                    <tr>\n
