<div class="section">\n            <h2>Key Design Patterns</h2>\n            \n            <div style="margin-bottom: 30px;">\n                <div class="arch-box">\n                    <strong>1. Mixin-Based Composition</strong> — Agent class uses 13 mixins for modular capabilities without deep inheritance hierarchies\n                </div>\n                <div class="arch-box">\n                    <strong>2. Callback-Driven Architecture</strong> — Agent execution feeds events (status, thinking, tool_output, approval) through callbacks for real-time monitoring\n                </div>\n                <div class="arch-box">\n                    <strong>3. Async-First Design</strong> — All I/O operations use asyncio with non-blocking patterns and thread pool execution\n                </div>\n                <div class="arch-box">\n                    <strong>4. Token-Aware Context Management</strong> — Multi-level token tracking with intelligent context compaction and message selection\n                </div>\n                <div class="arch-box">\n                    <strong>5. Multi-Layer Memory</strong> — Working (in-turn), Semantic (session-scoped), and Deep (long-term) memory for different retrieval patterns\n                </div>\n                <div class="arch-box">\n                    <strong>6. Guard Rails & Approval Workflows</strong> — Input/output guards with configurable levels for safe autonomous operation\n                </div>\n                <div class="arch-box">\n                    <strong>7. Scale Detection & Micro-Loops</strong> — Automatic detection of large-scale tasks triggers per-item processing with constant context\n                </div>\n                <div class="arch-box">\n                    <strong>8. Orchestration & Parallelization</strong> — DAG-based task decomposition with dependency constraints and timeout management\n                </div>\n                <div class="arch-box">\n                    <strong>9. File Registry & Cross-Task Sharing</strong> — Logical-to-physical path mapping for artifact discovery across tasks\n                </div>\n                <div class="arch-box">\n                    <strong>10. Configuration Hierarchy</strong> — Environment variables → .env → config.yaml (home) → config.yaml (local) → defaults\n                </div>\n            </div>\n        </div>\n\n        <!-- Technical Achievements -->\n        <div class="section">\n            <h2>Notable Technical Achievements</h2>\n            \n            <table>\n                <thead>\n                    <tr>\n                        <th>Achievement</th>\n                        <th>Description</th>\n                    </tr>\n                </thead>\n                <tbody>\n                    <tr>\n                        <td><strong>Token-Efficient Browser Automation</strong></td>\n                        <td>PinchTab uses accessibility trees (~800 tokens) instead of screenshots (~2K+ tokens), achieving 2-3x token efficiency</td>\n                    </tr>\n                    <tr>\n                        <td><strong>Chunked Processing Pipeline</strong></td>\n                        <td>Automatically detects context overflow and splits large documents into chunks for independent processing</td>\n                    </tr>\n                    <tr>\n                        <td><strong>Dual-Mode Orchestration</strong></td>\n                        <td>Supports both fast "loop" mode (direct tool execution) and "contracts" mode (planner + critic validation)</td>\n                    </tr>\n                    <tr>\n                        <td><strong>Intelligent Scale Detection</strong></td>\n                        <td>Automatically detects large-scale tasks and switches to per-item processing to prevent context explosion</td>\n                    </tr>\n                    <tr>\n                        <td><strong>Multi-Provider LLM Abstraction</strong></td>\n                        <td>Unified interface supporting Ollama, OpenAI, Anthropic, Gemini, xAI with provider-specific quirks handled transparently</td>\n temporal decay scoring for intelligent retrieval</td>\n                    </tr>\n                    <tr>\n                        <td><strong>Graceful Degradation</strong></td>\n <h4>Discord</h4>\n                    <p>DM-based polling interface with message normalization and audio file upload support</p>\n                </div>\n                <div class="card">\n                    <h4>Slack</h4>\n                    <p>DM-first polling with pagination, user caching, and thread reply support</p>\n                </div>\n                <div class="card">\n                    <h4>Google OAuth</h4>\n                    <p>PKCE-based authorization flow with token lifecycle management and credential injection</p>\n                </div>\n                <div </div>\n            </div>\n        </section>\n\n        <!-- Key Design Patterns -->\n        <section>\n            <h2>🎯 Key Design Patterns</h2>\n            \n            <div class="pattern-box">\n                <strong>1. Mixin-Based Composition</strong>\n                <p>13 specialized mixins provide distinct capabilities without deep inheritance hierarchies, enabling modular testing and feature toggling.</p>\n            </div>\n            \n            <div class="pattern-box">\n                <strong>2. Callback-Driven Architecture</strong>\n                <p>Agent execution feeds events through registered callbacks (status, thinking, tool_output, approval) that route to UI layers without tight coupling.</p>\n            </div>\n            \n            <div class="pattern-box">\n                <strong>3. Async-First Design</strong>\n                <p>All I/O operations use asyncio with non-blocking patterns. Long-running operations run in thread pools to prevent event loop blocking.</p>\n            </div>\n            \n            <div class="pattern-box">\n                <strong>4. Token-Aware Context Management</strong>\n                <p>System tracks token consumption at multiple levels and implements intelligent context compaction, chunking, and message selection.</p>\n            </div>\n            \n            <div class="pattern-box">\n                <strong>5. Multi-Layer Memory</strong>\n                <p>Working memory (in-turn), semantic memory (session-scoped), and deep memory (long-term) provide different retrieval patterns optimized for different timescales.</p>\n            </div>\n            \n            <div class="pattern-box">\n                <strong>6. Guard Rails & Approval Workflows</strong>\n                <p>Input/output guards with configurable levels enable safe autonomous operation with human oversight.</p>\n            </div>\n            \n            <div class="pattern-box">\n                <strong>7. Scale Detection & Micro-Loops</strong>\n                <p>Automatic detection of large-scale list-processing tasks triggers specialized micro-loop for per-item processing with constant context.</p>\n            </div>\n            \n            <div class="pattern-box">\n                <strong>8. Orchestration & Parallelization</strong>\n                <p>DAG-based task decomposition with parallel execution, dependency constraints, and timeout/retry policies for resilient workflows.</p>\n            </div>\n            \n            <div class="pattern-box">\n                <strong>9. File Registry & Cross-Task Sharing</strong>\n                <p>Logical-to-physical path mapping enables downstream tasks to discover and reference upstream artifacts seamlessly.</p>\n            </div>\n            \n            <div class="pattern-box">\n                <strong>10. Configuration Hierarchy</strong>\n                <p>Environment variables → .env file → config.yaml (home) → config.yaml (local) → hardcoded defaults provide flexible configuration.</p>\n            </div>\n        </section>\n\n        <!-- Technical Achievements -->\n        <section>\n            <h2>⭐ Notable Technical Achievements</h2>\n            \n            <div class="achievement">\n                <div class="achievement-title">1. Token-Efficient Browser Automation</div>\n                <p>PinchTab uses accessibility trees (~800 tokens) instead of screenshots (~2K+ tokens), achieving <span class="highlight">2-3x token efficiency</span> for web automation.</p>\n            </div>\n            \n            <div class="achievement">\n                <div class="achievement-title">2. Chunked Processing Pipeline</div>\n                <p>Automatically detects context overflow and splits large documents into chunks, processes independently, and combines results via LLM synthesis.</p>\n            </div>\n            \n            <div class="achievement">\n                <div class="achievement-title">3. Dual-Mode Orchestration</div>\n                <p>Supports both fast "loop" mode (direct tool execution) and "contracts" mode (planner + critic validation) for different task complexity levels.</p>\n            </div>\n            \n            <div class="achievement">\n                <div class="achievement-title">4. Intelligent Scale Detection</div>\n                <p>Automatically detects large-scale tasks and switches to per-item processing to prevent context explosion, with automatic list extraction after content fetch.</p>\n            </div>\n            \n            <div class="achievement">\n                <div class="achievement-title">5. Multi-Provider LLM Abstraction</div>\n                <p>Unified interface supporting Ollama, OpenAI, Anthropic, Gemini, xAI with provider-specific quirks handled transparently.</p>\n            </div>\n            \n            <div class="achievement">\n                <div class="achievement-title">6. Hybrid Memory Search</div>\n                <p>Combines full-text search (BM25) with vector embeddings and temporal decay scoring for intelligent context retrieval.</p>\n            </div>\n            \n            <div class="achievement">\n                <div class="achievement-title">7. Graceful Degradation</div>\n                <p>Every failure point has a fallback mechanism ensuring system resilience and continuous operation.</p>\n            </div>\n        </section>\n\n Reasoning Mixin</div>\n                    <div class="layer-content">Task contract generation, critic validation, and list-member extraction</div>\n                </div>\n                <div class="layer">\n                    <div class="layer-title">11. class="pattern-box">\n                <strong>1. Mixin-Based Composition</strong>\n                <p>13 specialized mixins provide distinct capabilities without deep inheritance hierarchies, enabling modular testing and feature toggling.</p>\n            </div>\n            \n            <div class="pattern-box">\n                <strong>2. Callback-Driven Architecture</strong>\n                <p>Agent execution feeds events through registered callbacks (status, thinking, tool_output, approval) that route to UI layers without tight coupling.</p>\n            </div>\n            \n            <div class="pattern-box">\n                <strong>3. Async-First Design</strong>\n                <p>All I/O operations use asyncio with non-blocking patterns. Long-running operations run in thread pools to prevent event loop blocking.</p>\n            </div>\n            \n            <div class="pattern-box">\n                <strong>4. Token-Aware Context Management</strong>\n                <p>System tracks token consumption at multiple levels and implements intelligent context compaction, chunking, and message selection.</p>\n            </div>\n            \n            <div class="pattern-box">\n                <strong>5. Multi-Layer Memory</strong>\n                <p>Working memory (in-turn), semantic memory (session-scoped), and deep memory (long-term) provide different retrieval patterns optimized for different timescales.</p>\n            </div>\n            \n            <div class="pattern-box">\n                <strong>6. Guard Rails & Approval Workflows</strong>\n                <p>Input/output guards with configurable levels enable safe autonomous operation with human oversight.</p>\n            </div>\n            \n            <div class="pattern-box">\n                <strong>7. Scale Detection & Micro-Loops</strong>\n                <p>Automatic detection of large-scale list-processing tasks triggers specialized micro-loop for per-item processing with constant context.</p>\n            </div>\n            \n            <div class="pattern-box">\n                <strong>8. Orchestration & Parallelization</strong>\n                <p>DAG-based task decomposition with parallel execution, dependency constraints, and timeout/retry policies for resilient workflows.</p>\n            </div>\n            \n            <div class="pattern-box">\n                <strong>9. File Registry & Cross-Task Sharing</strong>\n                <p>Logical-to-physical path mapping enables downstream tasks to discover and reference upstream artifacts seamlessly.</p>\n            </div>\n            \n            <div class="pattern-box">\n                <strong>10. Configuration Hierarchy</strong>\n                <p>Environment variables → .env file → config.yaml (home) → config.yaml (local) → hardcoded defaults provide flexible configuration.</p>\n            </div>\n        </section>\n\n        <!-- Technical Achievements -->\n        <section>\n            <h2>⭐ Notable Technical Achievements</h2>\n            \n            <div class="achievement">\n                <div class="achievement-title">1. Token-Efficient Browser Automation</div>\n                <p>PinchTab uses accessibility trees (~800 tokens) instead of screenshots (~2K+ tokens), achieving <span class="highlight">2-3x token efficiency</span> for web automation.</p>\n            </div>\n            \n            <div class="achievement">\n                <div class="achievement-title">2. Chunked Processing Pipeline</div>\n                <p>Automatically detects context overflow and splits large documents into chunks, processes independently, and combines results via LLM synthesis.</p>\n            </div>\n            \n            <div class="achievement">\n                <div class="achievement-title">3. Intelligent Scale Detection</div>\n                <p>Automatically detects large-scale tasks and switches to per-item processing to prevent context explosion, with automatic list extraction after content fetch.</p>\n            </div>\n            \n            <div class="achievement">\n                <div class="achievement-title">5. injection\n\n**BotPort** (`botport_client.py`):\n- Distributed coordination\n- Concern-based delegation\n- Multi-hop communication\n\n**Hotkey Daemon** (`hotkey_daemon.py`):\n- Global keyboard listener\n- Double/triple-tap state machine\n- Screenshot capture\n- Clipboard detection\n\n---\n\n## 🎯 Key Design Patterns\n\n### 1. Mixin-Based Composition\nThe Agent class uses 13 mixins to provide distinct capabilities without deep inheritance. Each mixin focuses on a specific concern, enabling modular testing and feature toggling.\n\n### 2. Callback-Driven Architecture\nAgent execution feeds events through registered callbacks (status, thinking, tool_output, approval) that route to UI layers without tight coupling. Enables real-time monitoring and multi-client synchronization.\n\n### 3. Async-First Design\nAll I/O operations use asyncio with non-blocking patterns. Long-running operations (LLM calls, file I/O, network requests) run in thread pools to prevent event loop blocking.\n\n### 4. Token-Aware Context Management\nThe system tracks token consumption at multiple levels (message, turn, session) and implements intelligent context compaction, chunking, and message selection to stay within LLM context windows.\n\n### 5. Multi-Layer Memory\nWorking memory (in-turn), semantic memory (session-scoped), and deep memory (long-term archive) provide different retrieval patterns optimized for recency, relevance, and scale.\n\n### 6. Guard Rails & Approval Workflows\nInput/output guards with configurable levels (stop_suspicious, ask_for_approval) and tool execution approval callbacks enable safe autonomous operation with human oversight.\n\n### 7. Scale Detection & Micro-Loops\nAutomatic detection of large-scale list-processing tasks triggers a specialized micro-loop that processes items one-at-a-time with constant context, preventing context window overflow.\n\n### 8. Orchestration & Parallelization\nSessionOrchestrator decomposes complex requests into DAGs, executes tasks in parallel with dependency constraints, and manages timeout/retry policies for resilient multi-step workflows.\n\n### 9. File Registry & Cross-Task Sharing\nFileRegistry maps logical paths to physical locations, enabling downstream tasks to discover and reference upstream artifacts without knowledge of session IDs or directory structures.\n\n### 10. Configuration Hierarchy\nEnvironment variables → .env file → config.yaml (home) → config.yaml (local) → hardcoded defaults provide flexible configuration with security-sensitive overrides.\n\n---\n\n## 🏆 Notable Technical Achievements\n\n### 1. Token-Efficient Browser Automation\n**PinchTab** uses accessibility trees (~800 tokens) instead of screenshots (~2K+ tokens), achieving **2-3x token efficiency** for web automation.\n\n### 2. Chunked Processing Pipeline\nAutomatically detects context overflow and splits large documents into chunks, processes independently, and combines results via LLM synthesis.\n\n### 3. Dual-Mode Orchestration\nSupports both fast "loop" mode (direct tool execution) and "contracts" mode (planner + critic validation) for different task complexity levels.\n\n### 4. Intelligent Scale Detection\nAutomatically detects large-scale tasks and switches to per-item processing to prevent context explosion, with automatic list extraction after content fetch.\n\n### 5. Multi-Provider LLM Abstraction\nUnified interface supporting Ollama, OpenAI, Anthropic, Gemini, xAI with provider-specific quirks (Anthropic caching, Gemini streaming issues) handled transparently.\n\n### 6. Hybrid Memory Search\nCombines full-text search (BM25) with vector embeddings and temporal decay scoring for intelligent context retrieval across multiple timescales.\n\n### 7. Graceful Degradation\nEvery failure point has a fallback (chunk LLM failure → skip chunk; combine overflow → concatenate; vision failure → return screenshot path).\n\n### 8. Encrypted Credential Management\nBrowser credentials stored with encryption, supports multiple auth types (bearer, api_key, basic, cookie), and automatic token refresh.\n\n### 9. Workflow Recording & Replay\nRecord user interactions in browser, parameterize with variables, and replay with different data. Uses resilient selectors (ARIA role → text → CSS) for durability.\n\n### 10. Real-Time Streaming\nWebSocket-based real-time streaming for chat, speech-to-text, and agent status updates with multi-client broadcast capability.\n\n---\n\n## 📊 System Metrics\n\n### Code Organization\n- **Core Agent:** 13 mixins + base Agent class\n- **Tools:** 40+ specialized tools across 8 categories\n- **Web Layer:** 50+ REST endpoints + WebSocket handlers\n- **Integrations:** 4 platform bridges\n- **Configuration:** 30+ subsystems\n- **Memory:** 3-layer architecture\n\n### Scalability Features\n- **Async I/O:** Non-blocking operations throughout\n- **Token Management:** Mixin-Based Composition\n**Pattern:** Agent class uses 13 mixins for distinct capabilities without deep inheritance hierarchies.\n```python\nclass Agent(\n    AgentOrchestrationMixin,\n    AgentToolLoopMixin,\n    AgentCompletionMixin,\n    # ... 10 more mixins\n):\n    pass\n```\n**Benefits:** Modular testing, feature toggling, clean separation of concerns.\n\n### 2. Callback-Driven Architecture\n**Pattern:** Agent execution feeds events through registered callbacks.\n```python\ncallbacks = {\n    \'status\': on_status,\n    \'thinking\': on_thinking,\n    \'tool_output\': on_tool_output,\n    \'approval\': on_approval\n}\n```\n**Benefits:** Real-time monitoring, multi-client synchronization, loose coupling.\n\n### 3. Async-First Design\n**Pattern:** All I/O operations use asyncio with non-blocking patterns.\n```python\nasync def execute_tool(tool_name, args):\n    return await tool_executor.run(tool_name, args)\n```\n**Benefits:** High concurrency, non-blocking event loop, scalable performance.\n\n### 4. Token-Aware Context Management\n**Pattern:** Track token consumption at message/turn/session levels.\n```python\nif current_tokens + message_tokens > max_context_tokens:\n    compact_context()  # Remove oldest messages\n```\n**Benefits:** Stay within LLM context windows, intelligent message selection.\n\n### 5. Multi-Layer Memory\n**Pattern:** Different retrieval patterns optimized for recency, relevance, scale.\n```\nWorking Memory (in-turn) → Semantic Memory (session) → Deep Memory (long-term)\n```\n**Benefits:** Fast access, intelligent retrieval, scalable knowledge storage.\n\n### 6. Guard Rails & Approval Workflows\n**Pattern:** Input/output guards with configurable approval levels.\n```python\nif guard_level == \'ask_for_approval\':\n    await request_human_approval(tool_call)\n```\n**Benefits:** Safe autonomous operation, human oversight, risk mitigation.\n\n### 7. Scale Detection & Micro-Loops\n**Pattern:** Automatic detection of large-scale tasks triggers specialized processing.\n```python\nif is_large_scale_list_task(request):\n    activate_scale_loop(items)  # Process one-at-a-time\n```\n**Benefits:** Prevent context overflow, constant-context isolation, scalability.\n\n### 8. Orchestration & Parallelization\n**Pattern:** DAG-based task decomposition with dependency resolution.\n```\nTask A (independent) ──┐\n                       ├─→ Task C (depends on A & B)\nTask B (independent) ──┘\n```\n**Benefits:** Parallel execution, timeout management, resilience.\n\n### 9. File Registry & Cross-Task Sharing\n**Pattern:** Logical-to-physical path mapping for artifact discovery.\n```python\nartifact = file_registry.lookup(\'report.pdf\')\n# Returns: /path/to/session/artifacts/report.pdf\n```\n**Benefits:** Cross-task sharing without session ID knowledge, artifact discovery.\n\n### 10. Configuration Hierarchy\n**Pattern:** Environment variables → .env → config.yaml (home) → config.yaml (local) → defaults.\n```\nEnvironment Variables (highest priority)\n    ↓\n.env file\n    ↓\nconfig.yaml (home directory)\n    ↓\nconfig.yaml (local directory)\n    ↓\nHardcoded Defaults (lowest priority)\n```\n**Benefits:** Flexible configuration, security-sensitive overrides, environment-specific settings.\n\n---\n\n## 🏆 NOTABLE TECHNICAL ACHIEVEMENTS\n\n### 1. Token-Efficient Browser Automation\n- **Problem:** Screenshots use ~2K+ tokens; context window overflow\n- **Solution:** PinchTab uses accessibility trees (~800 tokens)\n- **Result:** 2-3x token efficiency improvement\n\n### 2. Chunked Processing Pipeline\n- **Problem:** Large documents exceed context window\n- **Solution:** Auto-detect overflow, split into chunks, process independently, synthesize results\n- **Result:** Handle unlimited document sizes\n\n### 3. Dual-Mode Orchestration\n- **Problem:** Simple tasks need speed; complex tasks need planning\n- **Solution:** Fast "loop" mode (direct execution) + "contracts" mode (planner + critic)\n- **Result:** Optimal performance for all task complexities\n\n### 4. Intelligent Scale Detection\n- **Problem:** Large-scale tasks cause context explosion\n- **Solution:** Auto-detect large lists, switch to per-item processing\n- **Result:** Handle 1000+ items without context overflow\n\n### 5. Multi-Provider LLM Abstraction\n- **Problem:** Different LLM providers have different APIs and quirks\n- **Solution:** Unified interface with provider-specific handling\n- **Result:** Seamless provider switching (Ollama, OpenAI, Claude, Gemini, Grok)\n\n### 6. Hybrid Memory Search\n- **Problem:** Pure keyword search misses semantic relevance; pure vector search is slow\n- **Solution:** Combine BM25 + vector embeddings + temporal decay\n- **Result:** Intelligent context retrieval across multiple timescales\n\n### 7. Graceful Degradation\n- **Problem:** Single component failure breaks entire system\n- **Solution:** Fallbacks at every failure point\n- **Result:** Robust, resilient operation\n\n---\n\n## 📊 SYSTEM Application entry point | Arg parsing, TUI/web routing, signal handling |\n\n---\n\n## 🎨 KEY DESIGN PATTERNS\n\n### 1. Mixin-Based Composition\n**Pattern:** Agent class uses 13 mixins for distinct capabilities without deep inheritance hierarchies.\n```python\nclass Agent(\n    AgentOrchestrationMixin,\n    AgentToolLoopMixin,\n    AgentCompletionMixin,\n    # ... 10 more mixins\n):\n    pass\n```\n**Benefits:** Modular testing, feature toggling, clean separation of concerns.\n\n### 2. Callback-Driven Architecture\n**Pattern:** Agent execution feeds events through registered callbacks.\n```python\ncallbacks = {\n    \'status\': on_status,\n    \'thinking\': on_thinking,\n    \'tool_output\': on_tool_output,\n    \'approval\': on_approval\n}\n```\n**Benefits:** Real-time monitoring, multi-client synchronization, loose coupling.\n\n### 3. Async-First Design\n**Pattern:** All I/O operations use asyncio with non-blocking patterns.\n```python\nasync def execute_tool(tool_name, args):\n    return await tool_executor.run(tool_name, args)\n```\n**Benefits:** High concurrency, non-blocking event loop, scalable performance.\n\n### 4. Token-Aware Context Management\n**Pattern:** Track token consumption at message/turn/session levels.\n```python\nif current_tokens + message_tokens > max_context_tokens:\n    compact_context()  # Remove oldest messages\n```\n**Benefits:** Stay within LLM context windows, intelligent message selection.\n\n### 5. Multi-Layer Memory\n**Pattern:** Different retrieval patterns optimized for recency, relevance, scale.\n```\nWorking Memory (in-turn) → Semantic Memory (session) → Deep Memory (long-term)\n```\n**Benefits:** Fast access, intelligent retrieval, scalable knowledge storage.\n\n### 6. Guard Rails & Approval Workflows\n**Pattern:** Input/output guards with configurable approval levels.\n```python\nif guard_level == \'ask_for_approval\':\n    await request_human_approval(tool_call)\n```\n**Benefits:** Safe autonomous operation, human oversight, risk mitigation.\n\n### 7. Scale Detection & Micro-Loops\n**Pattern:** Automatic detection of large-scale tasks triggers specialized processing.\n```python\nif is_large_scale_list_task(request):\n    activate_scale_loop(items)  # Process one-at-a-time\n```\n**Benefits:** Prevent context overflow, constant-context isolation, scalability.\n\n### 8. Orchestration & Parallelization\n**Pattern:** DAG-based task decomposition with dependency resolution.\n```\nTask A (independent) ──┐\n                       ├─→ Task C (depends on A & B)\nTask B (independent) ──┘\n```\n**Benefits:** Parallel execution, timeout management, resilience.\n\n### 9. File Registry & Cross-Task Sharing\n**Pattern:** Logical-to-physical path mapping for artifact discovery.\n```python\nartifact = file_registry.lookup(\'report.pdf\')\n# Returns: /path/to/session/artifacts/report.pdf\n```\n**Benefits:** Cross-task sharing without session ID knowledge, artifact discovery.\n\n### 10. Configuration Hierarchy\n**Pattern:** Environment variables → .env → config.yaml (home) → config.yaml (local) → defaults.\n```\nEnvironment Variables (highest priority)\n    ↓\n.env file\n    ↓\nconfig.yaml (home directory)\n    ↓\nconfig.yaml (local directory)\n    ↓\nHardcoded Defaults (lowest priority)\n```\n**Benefits:** Flexible configuration, security-sensitive overrides, environment-specific settings.\n\n---\n\n## 🏆 NOTABLE TECHNICAL ACHIEVEMENTS\n\n### 1. Token-Efficient Browser Automation\n- **Problem:** Screenshots use ~2K+ tokens; context window overflow\n- **Solution:** PinchTab uses accessibility trees (~800 tokens)\n- **Result:** 2-3x token efficiency improvement\n\n### 2. Chunked Processing Pipeline\n- **Problem:** Large documents exceed context window\n- **Solution:** Auto-detect overflow, split into chunks, process independently, synthesize results\n- **Result:** Handle unlimited document sizes\n\n### 3. Dual-Mode Orchestration\n- **Problem:** Simple tasks need speed; complex tasks need planning\n- **Solution:** Fast "loop" mode (direct execution) + "contracts" mode (planner + critic)\n- **Result:** Optimal performance for all task complexities\n\n### 4. Intelligent Scale Detection\n- **Problem:** Large-scale tasks cause context explosion\n- **Solution:** Auto-detect large lists, switch to per-item processing\n- **Result:** Handle 1000+ items without context overflow\n\n### 5. Multi-Provider LLM Abstraction\n- **Problem:** Different LLM providers have different APIs and quirks\n- **Solution:** Unified interface with provider-specific handling\n- **Result:** Seamless provider switching (Ollama, OpenAI, Claude, Gemini, Grok)\n\n### 6. Hybrid Memory Search\n- **Problem:** Pure keyword search misses semantic relevance; pure vector search is slow\n- **Solution:** Combine BM25 + vector embeddings + temporal decay\n- **Result:** Intelligent context retrieval across multiple timescales\n\n### 7. Graceful Degradation\n- **Problem:** Single component failure breaks entire system\n- **Solution:** Fallbacks at every failure point\n- **Result:** Robust, resilient operation\n\n---\n\n## 📊 SYSTEM STATISTICS\n\n| Metric | Value |\n|--------|-------|\n| **Python Files** | 137 |\n| **Total Lines of Code** | 3,235,331 characters |\n| **Core Agent Mixins** | 13 |\n| **Integrated Tools** | 40+ |\n|
